    $(document).ready(function(){
    
        // https://developer.mozilla.org/it/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Math/random
        // Returns a random integer between min (included) and max (included)
        // Using Math.round() will give you a non-uniform distribution!
        function getRandomIntInclusive(min, max) {
            return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
        }
        
    
        // Define images to use
        var imgArray = ["http://media.ilgiornaledivicenza.it/media/attach/crociere/GDV2017/CROCIERA H9.gif",

     });

                                <div id="ajax-placeholder-69227068-1">
    <img src="http://www.ilgiornaledivicenza.it/gfx/siti/quotidiani_web-v3/images/spinners/ajax-loader.gif"
      style="display:block; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;">
    <script>
      (function(){
        var ajaxLoaded = false;

        function isScrolledIntoView(elem) {
          var $elem = $(elem);
          var $window = $(window);

          var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();
          var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();

          var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;
          var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height();

          return ((elemBottom <= docViewBottom) && (elemTop >= docViewTop));
        }

        function ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url) {
          ajaxLoaded = true;
          jQuery.get(url, function(data) {
            jQuery(ajaxId).replaceWith(data);
                      });
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
          var url = '\/multimedia-7.10195?ot=it.athesis.pagelayout.ajax.ot';
          var ajaxId = '#ajax-placeholder-69227068-1';
                    if (isScrolledIntoView($(ajaxId))) {
            ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url);
          } else {
            $(window).scroll(function() {
              var elem = $(ajaxId);
              if (!ajaxLoaded && isScrolledIntoView(elem)) {
                ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url);
              }
            })
          }
                  });
      })()
    </script>

    <script>
      (function(){
        var ajaxLoaded = false;

        function isScrolledIntoView(elem) {
          var $elem = $(elem);
          var $window = $(window);

          var docViewTop = $window.scrollTop();
          var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $window.height();

          var elemTop = $elem.offset().top;
          var elemBottom = elemTop + $elem.height();

          return ((elemBottom <= docViewBottom) && (elemTop >= docViewTop));
        }

        function ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url) {
          ajaxLoaded = true;
          jQuery.get(url, function(data) {
            jQuery(ajaxId).replaceWith(data);
                        jQuery(document).trigger('ajax-agenda-spalla');
                      });
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
          var url = '\/agenda-7.10192?ot=it.athesis.pagelayout.ajax.ot';
          var ajaxId = '#ajax-placeholder-69227639-1';
                    if (isScrolledIntoView($(ajaxId))) {
            ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url);
          } else {
            $(window).scroll(function() {
              var elem = $(ajaxId);
              if (!ajaxLoaded && isScrolledIntoView(elem)) {
                ajaxLoad(ajaxId, url);
              }
            })
          }
                  });
      })()
    </script>
